###xml 843 846 843 846 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 847 853 847 853 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 932 948 932 948 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g004">Figure 4K and 4L</xref>
###xml 1068 1084 1068 1084 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g004">Figure 4R and 4S</xref>
In addition to rotated stereociliary bundles in the sensory hair cells, strong patterning defects were also observed in Dvl3;LtapLp mutant cochleae. Separately, the patterning in the cochleae of Dvl3-/- and LtapLp/+ single mutants appeared normal (Figure 4M and 4N). However, the inner ears of Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ and Dvl3-/-;LtapLp/+ mutants with neural tube defects, were much smaller than in littermate controls (Figure 4O and 4P, respectively). Upon further dissection, the cochleae of the Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ and Dvl3-/-;LtapLp/+ mutants with craniorachischisis were also much shorter compared to controls (Figure 4M-P). At the cellular level, often in these Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ and Dvl3-/-;LtapLp/+ mutants the normal arrangement of 3 outer hair cell rows and 1 inner hair cell row was disrupted. In the apical region of Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ and Dvl3-/-;LtapLp/+ cochleae, additional rows of both outer and inner hair cells were observed (Figure 4K and 4L). Loss of outer hair cell rows was also detected in these mutants, so that the normal three rows became only two rows (Figure 4R and 4S). In total, this patterning defect was observed in 5-20% of the length of the cochlea.
###end p 38
###begin p 39
###xml 120 129 120 129 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g004">Figure 4T</xref>
###xml 145 154 145 154 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g004">Figure 4U</xref>
###xml 190 194 190 194 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 484 487 484 487 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
Finally, the location of Dvl3 expression was determined in the inner ear sensory organs, including both the vestibular (Figure 4T) and cochlear (Figure 4U) end organs, using the EYFP-tagged Dvl3 transgene. Dvl3-EYFP signals were asymmetrically localized in cells in all inner ear sensory regions. In the cochlea, Dvl3 was localized either on the lateral sides of the sensory hair cells, or on the medial side of the surrounding supporting cells, similar to what was observed for Dvl2 [6].
###end p 39
###begin title 40
###xml 37 41 37 41 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 41 44 41 44 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
No Skeletal Defects Were Observed in Dvl3-/- Mutants
###end title 40
###begin p 41
###xml 68 72 68 72 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 72 75 72 75 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 119 123 119 123 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 123 126 123 126 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 127 131 127 131 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 131 134 131 134 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 152 156 152 156 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Hamblet1">[40]</xref>
###xml 230 234 230 234 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 270 274 270 274 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 274 277 274 277 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 367 371 367 371 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 371 374 371 374 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
We have previously reported both vertebral and rib malformations in Dvl2-/-mutants and more severe skeletal defects in Dvl1-/-;Dvl2-/- double knockouts [40]. Given the overlapping expression patterns and high homology between the Dvls, we also examined the skeletons of Dvl3-/- mutants. However, no rib or vertebral abnormalities were observed (data not shown). 7/11 Dvl3-/- mutants showed xiphoid bifurication, but this was also observed in several wild type controls.
###end p 41
###begin title 42
###xml 14 18 14 18 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 19 23 19 23 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 28 32 28 32 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 33 37 33 37 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
Phenotypes of Dvl1;Dvl3 and Dvl2;Dvl3 Double Mutants
###end title 42
###begin p 43
###xml 19 23 19 23 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 28 32 28 32 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 65 69 65 69 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 69 72 69 72 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 73 77 73 77 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 77 80 77 80 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 157 160 157 160 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 171 175 171 175 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 176 180 176 180 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Hamblet1">[40]</xref>
###xml 221 225 221 225 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 244 248 244 248 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 279 283 279 283 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 284 288 284 288 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 293 297 293 297 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 298 302 298 302 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 324 328 324 328 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 328 331 328 331 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 332 336 332 336 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 336 339 336 339 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 344 348 344 348 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 348 351 348 351 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 352 356 352 356 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 356 359 356 359 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 448 452 448 452 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 452 455 452 455 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 456 460 456 460 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 460 463 460 463 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 485 501 485 501 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g005">Figure 5A and 5B</xref>
Redundancy between Dvl1 and Dvl2 was evident from our studies of Dvl1-/-;Dvl2-/- double mutants, which displayed novel phenotypes not observed in the single Dvl knockouts [38],[40]. To address possible redundancy between Dvl3 and the other two Dvls we examined the phenotypes of Dvl1;Dvl3 and Dvl2;Dvl3 double mutants. Both Dvl1+/-;Dvl3+/- and Dvl1-/-;Dvl3+/- mutants survived to adulthood and were fertile. Normal development was also observed in Dvl1-/-;Dvl3-/- embryos until E12.5 (Figure 5A and 5B), but these mutants died soon after of unknown causes, normally between E13.5 and E15.5. Importantly, no neural tube defects were observed.
###end p 43
###begin title 44
###xml 21 24 21 24 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
Phenotypes of double Dvl mutants at mid-gestation and late embryonic stages.
###end title 44
###begin p 45
###xml 35 39 35 39 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>

###xml 63 66 63 66 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 188 192 188 192 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 193 197 193 197 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 239 243 239 243 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 243 246 243 246 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 247 251 247 251 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 251 254 251 254 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 284 288 284 288 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 288 291 288 291 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 292 296 292 296 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 296 299 296 299 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 347 351 347 351 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 351 354 351 354 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 355 359 355 359 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 359 362 359 362 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 533 537 533 537 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 537 540 537 540 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 541 545 541 545 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 545 548 545 548 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
Normal development was observed in Dvl1-/- (A) and Dvl1-/-;Dvl3-/- mutants (B) at E10.5 (A,B), although these mutants die shortly after this stage, often between E13.5-15.5. Phenotypes of Dvl2;Dvl3 double mutants collected at E11.5 (C-H). Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- double heterozygotes (D) and Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants (G) appeared normal at this stage, but Dvl2-/-;Dvl3+/- mutants displayed craniorachishisis, severely abnormal hearts and posterior truncation and die at approximately E9.5 (H). Phenotypes of varying severity were observed in Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants at E18.5 (I-N). Most appeared shortened in the A-P axis, with abnormal head shape, shortened snout, and a kinked tail (K,L). Two mutants also displayed craniorachischisis and more severe A-P truncation and one of these further showed gastroschisis and absence of tail (M,N).
###end p 45
###begin p 46
###xml 17 21 17 21 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 21 24 21 24 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 25 29 25 29 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 29 32 29 32 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 37 41 37 41 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 41 44 41 44 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 45 49 45 49 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 49 52 49 52 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 88 103 88 103 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g005">Figure 5D and G</xref>
###xml 151 155 151 155 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 155 158 155 158 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 159 163 159 163 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 163 166 163 166 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 176 185 176 185 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g005">Figure 5H</xref>
###xml 370 373 370 373 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dv2</italic>
###xml 373 376 373 376 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 377 381 377 381 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 381 384 381 384 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
At mid-gestation Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- and Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- double mutants also appear normal (Figure 5D and G), however a striking phenotype was observed in Dvl2-/-;Dvl3+/- mutants (Figure 5H). These mutants do not appear to survive beyond E9.5 and display craniorachischisis, pericardial effusion and abnormal looping of the heart, as well as severe posterior truncation. No Dv2-/-;Dvl3-/- embryos have been recovered from litters collected from E8.5 onwards, suggesting lethality earlier in development.
###end p 46
###begin p 47
###xml 24 28 24 28 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 28 31 28 31 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 32 36 32 36 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 36 39 36 39 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 256 271 256 271 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g005">Figure 5K and L</xref>
###xml 318 322 318 322 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 322 325 322 325 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 326 330 326 330 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 330 333 330 333 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 474 490 474 490 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g005">Figure 5M and 5N</xref>
Defects are observed in Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- double mutants at later developmental stages. At E18.5 these mutants appear shorter along the anterior-posterior (A-P) axis, show an abnormal head shape and a truncated snout, as well as a shortened and kinked tail (Figure 5K and L). Craniorachischisis was also observed in two Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants. One of these with the neural tube defect also showed several other severe phenotypes, including gastroschisis and absence of tail (Figure 5M and 5N).
###end p 47
###begin title 48
###xml 19 23 19 23 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 24 28 24 28 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
Cardiac Defects in Dvl2;Dvl3 Double Mutants
###end title 48
###begin p 49
###xml 11 15 11 15 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 15 18 15 18 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 23 27 23 27 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 27 30 27 30 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 101 105 101 105 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 272 276 272 276 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 278 287 278 287 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g001">Figure 1E</xref>
###xml 293 297 293 297 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 299 308 299 308 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6A</xref>
Since both Dvl2-/- and Dvl3-/- mutants both display conotruncal defects, we determined whether these Dvls have redundant or distinct functions in heart development. As common spatial and temporal expression patterns may indicate similar functions, we first confirmed that Dvl3 (Figure 1E) and Dvl2 (Figure 6A) shared comparable expression patterns in the heart at E9.5 during conotruncal development.
###end p 49

Deconvolution microscopy image showing EGFP-Dvl2 BAC transgene expression in the heart at E9.5 (A). Three (I,J) appeared similar to Dvl3-/- mutants (G,H), two had a 'medium' phenotype, which was worse than Dvl3-/- mutants (K,L) and two had a much worsened phenotype compared to Dvl3-/- mutants with severely altered morphology (M,N).

###begin p 52
###xml 32 36 32 36 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 36 39 36 39 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>

###xml 44 47 44 47 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 182 186 182 186 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 191 195 191 195 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 214 218 214 218 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 218 221 218 221 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 222 226 222 226 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 226 229 226 229 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 358 362 358 362 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 362 365 362 365 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 366 370 366 370 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 370 373 370 373 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 400 409 400 409 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6B</xref>
###xml 460 471 460 471 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6C&#8211;F</xref>
###xml 230 234 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
We first examined the hearts of Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- double heterozygotes to see whether these mutants had similar defects as the homozygotes, which would suggest redundant functions for Dvl2 and Dvl3. We observed that Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- mice often survive to adulthood and are fertile. However, in an inbred background, conotruncal abnormalities were seen in 11/28 Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- hearts examined at E18.5 (Figure 6B). These defects included 9 DORV, 1 PTA and 1 TGA (Figure 6C-F).
###end p 52
###begin p 53
###xml 14 18 14 18 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 18 21 18 21 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>

###xml 249 253 249 253 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 253 256 253 256 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 265 281 265 281 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6G and 6H</xref>

###xml 330 333 330 333 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>

###xml 472 483 472 483 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6K&#8211;N</xref>
###xml 615 631 615 631 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6K and 6L</xref>
###xml 648 652 648 652 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 652 655 652 655 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 656 660 656 660 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 660 663 660 663 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 709 713 709 713 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 713 716 713 716 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 785 801 785 801 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6M and 6N</xref>
###xml 908 924 908 924 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g006">Figure 6M and 6N</xref>
The hearts of Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants were also examined to determine whether an extra loss of one copy of Dvl2 would worsen the phenotype of Dvl3-/- mutants. Three Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- hearts collected at P0 (Figure 6I and 6J) had similar morphology to Dvl3-/- hearts (Figure 6G and 6H), 1 with DORV and 2 with PTA. However, four Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- hearts collected appeared to have a worse phenotype than Dvl3-/- mutants with varying degrees of severity and all displaying PTA (Figure 6K-N). Two were slightly smaller and had lost the characteristic fist shape heart morphology, becoming less tapered towards the bottom (Figure 6K and 6L). The other two Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- hearts were much reduced in size compared to Dvl3-/- mutants and had severely altered morphology, with a teardrop shape (Figure 6M and 6N). The embryos that the hearts were collected from were all alive, apart from the two severest phenotypes (Figure 6M and 6N), which were dead. After sectioning, it appeared that both right and left ventricles were still present in all samples.
###end p 53

###xml 988 991 988 991 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1035 1044 1035 1044 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g007">Figure 7D</xref>
###xml 1056 1060 1056 1060 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1060 1063 1060 1063 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1064 1070 1064 1070 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1TG</italic>
###xml 1177 1183 1177 1183 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1TG</italic>
###xml 1212 1216 1212 1216 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1216 1219 1216 1219 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1288 1292 1288 1292 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1292 1295 1292 1295 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1349 1352 1349 1352 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 992 996 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 1296 1300 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
The generation of fully functional Dvl transgenes (here and in [6]) allowed us to use a genetic approach to further determine redundancy of function between the Dvl proteins during development. We determined whether an extra copy of either Dvl1 or Dvl2, in the form of Dvl1-ECFP and Dvl2-EGFP BAC transgenes (which we will refer to here as Dvl1TG and Dvl2TG, respectively) was able to rescue the lethal Dvl3-/- phenotype. Importantly, western blot analysis revealed that none of the Dvl transgenes were overexpressed compared to protein levels from wild type alleles (Figure 7A-C). As shown above, Dvl3-/- mutants (which still have 2 copies of the Dvl1 allele and 2 copies of the Dvl2 allele) cannot survive. Surprisingly, we found that addition of the Dvl1TG rescued the Dvl3-/- phenotype such that Dvl3-/-;Dvl1TG mutants (now Dvl3-/- with 3 copies of Dvl1 and 2 copies of Dvl2) survived. To test whether this was a complete rescue, we crossed these viable Dvl3-/-;Dvl1TG mutants to Dvl3+/- mice and genotyped the progeny at weaning (Figure 7D). Eighteen Dvl3-/-;Dvl1TG rescued animals were recovered, compared to 16 that would be expected from normal Mendelian ratios if the Dvl1TG is fully able to rescue the Dvl3-/- phenotype. As these crosses were performed in a mixed background, 4 Dvl3-/- mice also survived with out an extra copy of another Dvl gene.
###end p 55
###begin title 56
###xml 41 44 41 44 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 80 84 80 84 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
Genetic crosses to demonstrate rescue of Dvl mutants with extra copies of other Dvls.
###end title 56
###begin p 57
###xml 60 78 60 78 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1-ECFP (Dvl1TG)</italic>
###xml 83 92 83 92 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2-EGFP</italic>
###xml 94 100 94 100 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 134 138 134 138 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 138 141 138 141 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 489 493 489 493 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 496 500 496 500 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 500 503 500 503 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 504 510 504 510 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1TG</italic>
###xml 541 543 541 543 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/</sup>
###xml 537 543 537 543 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3<sup>+/</sup></italic>
###xml 543 544 543 544 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;</sup>
###xml 629 635 629 635 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 696 714 696 714 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1-ECFP (Dvl1TG)</italic>
###xml 719 737 719 737 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3-EYFP (Dvl3TG)</italic>
###xml 797 801 797 801 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 805 809 805 809 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 823 827 823 827 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 827 830 827 830 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 946 950 946 950 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 950 953 950 953 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 954 958 954 958 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 958 961 958 961 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 988 992 988 992 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 992 995 992 995 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 996 1002 996 1002 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 1067 1073 1067 1073 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 545 549 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
A genetic approach was used to determine the ability of the Dvl1-ECFP (Dvl1TG) and Dvl2-EGFP (Dvl2TG) BAC transgenes to rescue lethal Dvl3-/- phenotype. Western blot analysis showing relative levels of Dvl1-ECFP (A), Dvl2-EGFP (B) and Dvl3-EYFP (C) compared to protein levels from wild type alleles. Two Dvl2-EGFP transgenes are shown, one representing wild type Dvl2 (left, Dvl2) and one with and a single point mutation that interrupts signaling through the PCP pathway (right, Dvl2-dsh1[38]). Dvl3-/-;Dvl1TG mutants were crossed with Dvl3+/- mice and the progeny genotyped at weaning (D). A similar cross was set up using the Dvl2TG and the experiment repeated (E). Parallel crosses using the Dvl1-ECFP (Dvl1TG) and Dvl3-EYFP (Dvl3TG) were also set up to determine whether additional copies of Dvl1 or Dvl3 could rescue Dvl2-/- lethality (F and G, respectively). To confirm that the BAC transgenes were behaving analogous to wild type alleles Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- mutants were crossed with Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mutants and the surviving progeny were genotyped to test if the Dvl2TG could still rescue (H).
###end p 57
###begin p 58
###xml 44 50 44 50 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 70 74 70 74 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 74 77 74 77 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 132 136 132 136 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 162 166 162 166 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 166 169 166 169 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 170 176 170 176 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 190 194 190 194 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 194 197 194 197 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 243 252 243 252 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g007">Figure 7E</xref>
###xml 265 269 265 269 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 269 272 269 272 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 273 279 273 279 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 383 387 383 387 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 387 390 387 390 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 424 428 424 428 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 198 202 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 280 284 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
Interestingly, in a similar cross using the Dvl2TG, we found that the Dvl3-/- lethal phenotype was also rescued by an extra copy of Dvl2. We crossed these viable Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mutants with Dvl3+/- mice and genotyped the offspring at weaning (Figure 7E). Seventeen Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mice were recovered, out of 19 expected from a full rescue, indicating approximately 90% rescue of the Dvl3-/- lethal phenotype with additional Dvl2.
###end p 58
###begin p 59
###xml 10 14 10 14 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>

###xml 624 627 624 627 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 663 666 663 666 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 706 712 706 712 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1TG</italic>
###xml 736 740 736 740 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 740 743 740 743 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 753 762 753 762 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g007">Figure 7G</xref>
###xml 213 217 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 460 464 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
As 50% of Dvl2-/- mutants die perinatally, we used a similar strategy to determine whether additional copies of Dvl1 or Dvl3 could rescue Dvl2-/- lethality. From crosses between Dvl2-/-;Dvl3TG mutants and Dvl2+/- mice, 24 Dvl2-/-;Dvl3TG mutants survived, out of 25 expected from a full rescue, indicating approximately 96% rescue of the Dvl2-/- phenotype with an extra copy of Dvl3 (Figure 7F). However, from crosses between Dvl2-/-;Dvl1TG mutants and Dvl2+/- mice, only 10 Dvl2-/-;Dvl1TG mutants were recovered, out of 18 expected from Mendelian ratios if the Dvl1TG was able to rescue the Dvl2-/- phenotype. As 50% of Dvl2-/- mutants survive without additional Dvl copies, this indicates that adding the Dvl1TG was not able to rescue Dvl2-/- mutants (Figure 7G).
###end p 59

###xml 430 439 430 439 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g007">Figure 7H</xref>
###xml 449 453 449 453 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 453 456 453 456 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/+</sup>
###xml 457 461 457 461 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 461 464 461 464 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 465 471 465 471 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 511 515 511 515 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 540 544 540 544 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 647 651 647 651 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 651 654 651 654 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 655 659 655 659 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 659 662 659 662 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 663 669 663 669 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 758 764 758 764 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 805 809 805 809 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 852 856 852 856 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 860 864 860 864 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 864 867 864 867 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 868 872 868 872 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 872 875 872 875 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 876 882 876 882 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 960 966 960 966 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 981 985 981 985 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 985 988 985 988 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1135 1139 1135 1139 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1139 1142 1139 1142 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
To confirm that the BAC transgenes were actually behaving as wild type alleles and that ectopic or inappropriate expression levels were not responsible for rescuing the mutant phenotypes, we genetically reduced the Dvl gene dosage by introducing a knock-out Dvl allele and again tested the rescue ability of the transgene. Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- mutants were crossed with Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mutants and the surviving progeny were genotyped (Figure 7H). Twelve Dvl2+/+;Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mutants with both wild type alleles of Dvl2 (a total of 3 copies of Dvl2) survived, comparable to 9 expected from normal Mendelian ratios, indicating full rescue. However, no Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mutants were recovered, even though 9 were expected from normal Mendelian ratios if the Dvl2TG could still rescue. Thus, correction of Dvl2 dosage from three copies to two copies of Dvl2 in Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mutants (1 wild type allele and the transgene) eliminated the ability of the Dvl2TG to rescue the Dvl3-/- mutant phenotype, supporting the conclusion that ectopic expression or over-expression of the transgene was not responsible for the rescue of the Dvl3-/- phenotype.
###end p 60

###xml 20 24 20 24 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>

###xml 893 897 893 897 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>

###xml 901 905 901 905 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 905 908 905 908 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 942 946 942 946 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 955 968 955 968 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g008">Figure 8C,H,M</xref>
###xml 1042 1051 1042 1051 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g008">Figure 8H</xref>
###xml 1061 1065 1061 1065 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 1065 1068 1065 1068 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1069 1073 1069 1073 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1073 1076 1073 1076 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1156 1169 1156 1169 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g008">Figure 8D,I,N</xref>
###xml 1448 1457 1448 1457 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g008">Figure 8N</xref>
###xml 1528 1532 1528 1532 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 1532 1535 1532 1535 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1536 1540 1536 1540 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1540 1543 1540 1543 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1582 1586 1582 1586 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1586 1589 1586 1589 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1600 1611 1600 1611 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g008">Figure 8P,Q</xref>
Similar cochlear defects have been observed in both Dvl1-/-;Dvl2-/-[6] and Dvl3-/- mutants (Figure 4). Therefore, we examined whether all three Dvls have redundant functions in the developing organ of Corti. The inner ears of double Dvl mutants were studied to determine whether the further loss of an additional Dvl gene would worsen the phenotype observed in Dvl3-/- mutants. Only the cochlea from Dvl1-/-;Dvl3+/-, Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- and Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants were examined as other double Dvl mutants were lethal too early in development. The organ of Corti from Dvl1-/-;Dvl3+/- mutants appeared normal (data not shown), as did those from the Dvl2+/- (Figure 8A,F,K) and Dvl3+/- (not shown) single heterozygote samples. However, several of the sensory hair cells in Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- double heterozygotes had rotated stereociliary bundles (Figure 8B,G,L). This phenotype appeared worse in the Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants with the loss of another Dvl3 allele (Figure 8C,H,M) and mild patterning defects were also observed in one of these mutants (Figure 8H). In the Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants that displayed craniorachischisis, the phenotype was even more severe (Figure 8D,I,N). Throughout the whole cochlea duct the hair cells did not appear to be fully developed, even in the basal region. Additionally, it is hard to see the typical shape of stereociliary bundles in most of the hair cells and the differentiation of these cells is apparently delayed (Figure 8N). Strong patterning defects were also observed as the cochleae of the Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants were much shorter compared to Dvl3-/- controls (Figure 8P,Q).
###end p 62

###xml 29 33 29 33 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 87 91 87 91 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>

###xml 120 129 120 129 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2-EGFP</italic>

###xml 173 179 173 179 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2TG</italic>
###xml 272 285 272 285 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g008">Figure 8E,J,O</xref>
###xml 327 331 327 331 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 331 334 331 334 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 344 352 344 352 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g004">Figure 4</xref>
###xml 401 405 401 405 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 474 478 474 478 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 478 481 478 481 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
Functional redundancy of the Dvls in cochlea development could only be examined in the Dvl3-/- mutants rescued with the Dvl2-EGFP transgene. The organ of Corti from Dvl3-/-;Dvl2TG mutants still displayed misorientation of stereocilia in several of the sensory hair cells (Figure 8E,J,O), similar to the phenotype described for Dvl3-/- mutants (Figure 4), indicating that increasing the copy number of Dvl2 was not able to restore the correct alignment of stereocilia in the Dvl3-/- mutants.
###end p 65
###begin title 66
###xml 27 30 27 30 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
Canonical Wnt Signaling in Dvl Mutants
###end title 66
###begin p 67
###xml 30 33 30 33 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
###xml 34 38 34 38 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 286 290 283 287 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LacZ</italic>
###xml 389 392 386 389 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 513 516 510 513 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 581 592 578 589 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g009">Figure 9A&#8211;C</xref>
###xml 604 615 601 612 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g009">Figure 9D&#8211;F</xref>
###xml 685 688 682 685 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 697 701 694 698 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 701 704 698 701 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 705 709 702 706 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 709 712 706 709 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 714 718 711 715 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 718 721 715 718 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 722 726 719 723 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 726 729 723 726 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 731 734 728 731 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dv2</italic>
###xml 734 737 731 734 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 738 742 735 739 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 742 745 739 742 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 747 751 744 748 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 751 754 748 751 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 755 759 752 756 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 759 762 756 759 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 767 771 764 768 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 771 774 768 771 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 775 779 772 776 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 779 782 776 779 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 792 803 789 800 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g009">Figure 9G&#8211;I</xref>
###xml 911 915 908 912 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 915 918 912 915 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 928 937 925 934 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g009">Figure 9A</xref>
###xml 962 966 959 963 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 966 969 963 966 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 979 988 976 985 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g009">Figure 9B</xref>
###xml 1088 1092 1085 1089 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 1092 1095 1089 1092 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1111 1120 1108 1117 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g009">Figure 9E</xref>
###xml 242 246 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 1096 1100 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
Previous studies from our lab [6],[38] and data presented above are consistent with a role for the Dvls in the PCP pathway during neurulation and cochlear development, while a role for Dvls in Wnt signaling is not as clear. Therefore, BATgal mice, which carry a beta-catenin-responsive LacZ gene, were used to determine whether canonical Wnt signaling was functional or interrupted in the Dvl mutants during mid-gestation. Global canonical Wnt signaling patterns appeared largely unaffected in each of the single Dvl mutants compared to their wild type littermates at either E9.5 (Figure 9A-C) or E11.5 (Figure 9D-F). Canonical Wnt signaling was also generally unchanged in the double Dvl mutants Dvl1-/-;Dvl2-/-, Dvl1-/-;Dvl3-/-, Dv2+/-;Dvl3+/-, Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- and Dvl2-/-;Dvl3+/- at E9.5 (Figure 9G-I). However, subtle abnormalities were observed. For example, TCF activity appears reduced in the somites of Dvl1-/- mutants (Figure 9A) and in the limb bud of Dvl2-/- mutants (Figure 9B) at E9.5, and the pattern of staining appears altered in both the somites and pharyngeal region of Dvl2-/- mice at E11.5 (Figure 9E).
###end p 67

###xml 34 37 34 37 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
Canonical Wnt signaling in double Dvl mutants at mid-gestation.

###xml 342 346 342 346 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>

###xml 361 364 361 364 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>

Double Dvl mutants; Dvl1-/-;Dvl2-/- (G), Dvl1-/-;Dvl3-/- (H) and Dv2+/-;Dvl3+/-, Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- and Dvl2-/-;Dvl3+/- (I) with the reporter were isolated at E9.5, with suitable control littermates.
