###begin title 70
Discussion
###end title 70
###begin p 71
###xml 164 168 164 168 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Axelrod1">[42]</xref>
###xml 169 173 169 173 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Boutros1">[43]</xref>
###xml 183 187 183 187 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wallingford2">[37]</xref>
###xml 189 193 189 193 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Rothbacher1">[44]</xref>
###xml 194 198 194 198 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wallingford4">[46]</xref>
###xml 206 209 206 209 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
###xml 210 214 210 214 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 240 244 240 244 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Lee1">[47]</xref>
###xml 245 249 245 249 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Zeng1">[49]</xref>
###xml 628 636 628 636 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vitro</italic>
###xml 636 640 636 640 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Lee1">[47]</xref>
###xml 720 727 720 727 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 770 774 770 774 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 779 783 779 783 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 809 813 809 813 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 814 818 814 818 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Hamblet1">[40]</xref>
###xml 819 823 819 823 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Lijam2">[41]</xref>
###xml 877 881 877 881 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 975 982 975 982 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 1031 1034 1031 1034 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 1089 1093 1089 1093 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 1113 1120 1113 1120 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">in vivo</italic>
###xml 1160 1163 1160 1163 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 1175 1178 1175 1178 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 1199 1208 1199 1208 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="fig" rid="pgen-1000259-g010">Figure 10</xref>
###xml 153 163 <span type="species:ncbi:7227">Drosophila</span>
###xml 200 205 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mouse</span>
###xml 1042 1046 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
A large body of evidence demonstrates that Dvl proteins function in highly conserved pathways in both vertebrates and invertebrates. It is known that in Drosophila [42],[43], Xenopus [37], [44]-[46], mouse [6],[38] and mammalian cell lines [47]-[49], Dishevelled proteins mediate their effects on the canonical and non-canonical Wnt pathways via highly conserved protein domains. As essential components of both the canonical Wnt and PCP pathways, Dvl proteins are required for many developmental processes. A recent publication has addressed the possibility of redundancy between the three Dvl proteins in mammalian cell lines in vitro[47]. We further aim to determine the action of the Dvl proteins during development in vivo. Having previously described the roles of Dvl1 and Dvl2 in mammalian development [38],[40],[41], we now describe the specific developmental roles of Dvl3 and additionally use well-established genetic approaches to determine the pathways disrupted in vivo that account for the phenotypes observed in the Dvl mutant mice and to demonstrate redundancy between the Dvls during development in vivo. A summary of the phenotypes of single Dvl and double Dvl mutants is shown in Figure 10.
###end p 71
###begin title 72
###xml 36 39 36 39 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 51 54 51 54 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
Summary of the phenotypes of single Dvl and double Dvl mutants.
###end title 72
###begin p 73
###xml 7 10 7 10 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 117 120 117 120 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 175 178 175 178 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
Single Dvl mutants display distinct phenotypes, but both novel and more severe phenotypes are observed in the double Dvl mutants, indicating functional redundancy between the Dvl genes.
###end p 73
###begin p 74
###xml 0 4 0 4 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 252 256 252 256 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Chien1">[50]</xref>
###xml 257 261 257 261 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Srivastava2">[51]</xref>
###xml 275 279 275 279 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 350 354 350 354 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 354 358 354 358 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Hamblet1">[40]</xref>
###xml 510 514 510 514 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 519 523 519 523 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 616 620 616 620 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 620 623 620 623 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 624 628 624 628 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 628 631 628 631 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 679 683 679 683 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 683 686 683 686 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 691 695 691 695 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 695 698 695 698 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 783 787 783 787 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 787 790 787 790 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 791 795 791 795 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 795 798 795 798 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 803 807 803 807 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 807 810 807 810 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 811 815 811 815 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 815 818 815 818 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 853 857 853 857 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 857 860 857 860 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 865 869 865 869 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 869 872 869 872 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 925 929 925 929 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 1023 1027 1023 1027 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 1031 1035 1031 1035 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 1054 1063 1054 1063 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1-ECFP</italic>
###xml 1067 1076 1067 1076 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2-EGFP</italic>
###xml 1112 1116 1112 1116 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1116 1119 1116 1119 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1171 1175 1171 1175 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 1180 1184 1180 1184 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 1215 1219 1215 1219 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 14 18 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
Dvl3 knockout mice die perinatally with cardiac outflow defects, indicating an important role for Dvl3 in conotruncal development. This is particularly interesting as approximately 30% of all congenital heart diseases are due to defects in this region [50],[51]. The loss of Dvl3 causes a similar conotruncal phenotype to those observed with loss of Dvl2[40], suggesting redundant functions for these homologous genes in outflow tract development. This was supported both by the similar expression patterns of Dvl2 and Dvl3 found during conotruncal development and the observation of cardiac abnormalities in double Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- heterozygotes, as compared to normal hearts of Dvl2+/- and Dvl3+/- single heterozygotes. The increased severity of the cardiac phenotype of the double Dvl2-/-;Dvl3+/- and Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants, compared with the single Dvl2-/- and Dvl3-/- mutants, further indicates redundancy between these Dvls in heart development. Finally, with a genetic approach we found that an extra copy of either Dvl1 or Dvl2, using either the Dvl1-ECFP or Dvl2-EGFP BAC transgene, could rescue lethal Dvl3-/- heart phenotype, demonstrating the ability of both Dvl1 and Dvl2 to compensate for the loss of Dvl3 to enable normal development.
###end p 74
###begin p 75
###xml 23 27 23 27 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 60 64 60 64 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 69 73 69 73 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 142 146 142 146 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 173 177 173 177 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 177 180 177 180 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 752 756 752 756 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Lee1">[47]</xref>
Our data suggests that Dvl1 shares redundant functions with Dvl2 and Dvl3 in cardiac development. However we found that an additional copy of Dvl1 is not able to rescue the Dvl2-/- cardiac defects. Although the Dvl proteins appear to have the same expression patterns and redundant functions, we have not yet addressed the possibility of differences in protein expression level. There may a certain threshold of Dvl protein required for normal heart development, but under this threshold there is insufficient signaling to permit normal development. Interestingly, a recent paper by Lee et al. demonstrated that in a number of mammalian cell lines all three Dvls are present, but that the relative levels of expression of the three Dvls differ greatly [47].
###end p 75
###begin p 76
###xml 331 336 331 336 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Pitx2</italic>
###xml 336 340 336 340 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Kioussi1">[52]</xref>
###xml 421 425 421 425 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
Normal development of the outflow tract requires the addition of cells from both the CNC and the SHF, and a lack of contribution of either of these tissues is often the cause of defects in the conotruncal region. Further, Dvl2 has previously been found to be important for controlling proliferation of CNC cells, via activation of Pitx2[52]. However, both CNC cells and SHF cells appeared to be present in the absence of Dvl3, suggesting that the heart defects are not due to a complete lack of either of these tissues. Further studies to determine whether these cells are properly situated in relation to the surrounding tissues, and whether they are indeed still functional, are in progress.
###end p 76
###begin p 77
###xml 182 186 182 186 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 186 189 186 189 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 335 339 335 339 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Ai1">[19]</xref>
###xml 340 344 340 344 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Lin1">[23]</xref>
###xml 531 535 531 535 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 535 538 535 538 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 539 545 539 545 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 624 628 624 628 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 190 194 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
Dvl proteins function in both the canonical and non-canonical PCP pathways, therefore disruption of either or both of these pathways could be the cause of the phenotypes observed in Dvl3-/- mice. Roles for both pathways in heart development have been reported. Canonical Wnt signals appear essential for the proliferation of SHF cells [19]-[23], whereas the PCP pathway is thought to be necessary for the polarized migration of myocardial cells required in the outflow tract septum (Henderson et al., 2006; Phillips et al., 2005). Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ double heterozygotes displayed no abnormal heart phenotype, suggesting that Dvl3 may function through the canonical and not the PCP pathway during heart development. Conversely, it is possible that the level of PCP signaling was not reduced below the hypothetical threshold required for the phenotype. Further experiments will be required to distinguish these possibilities.
###end p 77
###begin p 78
###xml 155 159 155 159 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 224 228 224 228 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 247 251 247 251 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 256 260 256 260 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 260 264 260 264 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 287 290 287 290 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 366 370 366 370 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 375 379 375 379 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 383 387 383 387 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 392 396 392 396 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 404 408 404 408 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 408 411 408 411 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 412 416 412 416 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 416 419 416 419 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 421 425 421 425 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 425 428 425 428 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 429 433 429 433 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 433 436 433 436 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 438 442 438 442 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 442 445 442 445 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 446 450 446 450 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 450 453 450 453 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 586 590 586 590 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 590 593 590 593 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 594 598 594 598 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 598 601 598 601 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 673 677 673 677 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 748 751 748 751 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 778 784 778 784 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 792 796 792 796 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 796 799 796 799 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 800 806 800 806 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 811 815 811 815 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 815 818 815 818 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 819 825 819 825 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 832 836 832 836 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 836 839 836 839 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 840 846 840 846 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 891 895 891 895 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 919 925 919 925 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Vangl2</italic>
###xml 949 953 949 953 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 785 789 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
We have shown here that Dvl1 and Dvl3 colocalize in the developing neural tube with similar expression patterns to that of Dvl2 as we described previously [38], and provide further evidence for a similar functional role for Dvl3 in neurulation as Dvl1 and Dvl2[38]. Although none of the Dvl single knockouts display neural tube closure defects, disruption of either Dvl1 and Dvl2 or Dvl2 and Dvl3 genes (Dvl1-/-;Dvl2-/-, Dvl2-/-;Dvl3+/-, Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/-) results in incomplete neurulation, suggesting a dosage sensitive redundant role for all three Dvls in this process. Interestingly, Dvl1-/-;Dvl3-/- mutants did not display neural tube defects, suggesting that the three Dvls are not functionally equivalent. Neural tube defects appear in single Dvl mutants when crossed with LtapLp mice, (Dvl2-/-;LtapLp/+ , Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ and Dvl3-/-;LtapLp/+), indicating genetic interaction with the Dvls and the PCP component, Vangl2 and therefore that the Dvls signal through the PCP pathway to promote neural tube closure.
###end p 78
###begin p 79
###xml 79 83 79 83 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 84 90 84 90 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 264 268 264 268 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wallingford5">[53]</xref>
###xml 377 381 377 381 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Simons1">[54]</xref>
###xml 425 429 425 429 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Ross1">[55]</xref>
###xml 532 540 532 540 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">inturned</italic>
###xml 545 550 545 550 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">fuzzy</italic>
###xml 554 568 554 568 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Xenopus laevis</italic>
###xml 648 652 648 652 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Park1">[56]</xref>
###xml 675 686 675 686 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">dishevelled</italic>
###xml 691 699 691 699 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">inturned</italic>
###xml 804 808 804 808 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Park1">[56]</xref>
###xml 554 568 <span type="species:ncbi:8355">Xenopus laevis</span>
It is interesting that both exencephaly and craniorachischisis are observed in Dvl3;LtapLp mutants. Craniorachischisis has been observed in many mutants with disrupted PCP signaling, whereas exencephaly is often associated with defective ciliogenesis (reviewed in [53]). Recently a connection between cilia and PCP signaling has been suggested as the ciliary proteins Inversin [54] and Bardet-Biedl Syndrome protein-4 (BBS4) [55] were shown to influence PCP signaling and CE movements. Additionally, disruption of the PCP effectors inturned and fuzzy in Xenopus laevis demonstrated a link between ciliogenesis, PCP signaling and Hedgehog signaling [56]. Localization of both dishevelled and inturned near the basal apparatus of cilia further suggests a role for PCP components in regulating ciliogenesis [56].
###end p 79
###begin p 80
###xml 33 37 33 37 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 37 40 37 40 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 118 124 118 124 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 151 155 151 155 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 183 189 183 189 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Vangl2</italic>
###xml 420 424 420 424 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 425 431 425 431 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 654 657 654 657 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
###xml 699 703 699 703 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang2">[34]</xref>
###xml 704 708 704 708 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Deans1">[57]</xref>
###xml 709 713 709 713 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Montcouquiol2">[58]</xref>
###xml 838 842 838 842 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Klein1">[59]</xref>
###xml 843 847 843 847 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Strutt1">[60]</xref>
###xml 1031 1035 1031 1035 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Jones1">[32]</xref>
###xml 1396 1399 1396 1399 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
The polarity defects observed in Dvl3-/- cochleae were much more severe with the introduction of an additional single LtapLp mutation, indicating that Dvl3 genetically interacts with Vangl2 and functions in the PCP pathway to regulate cell polarity in the organ of Corti. The CE movements driven by the PCP pathway that are required for the extension and thinning of the developing organ of Corti were also disrupted in Dvl3;LtapLp mutants, resulting in shortened organs of Corti relative to controls. Furthermore, the asymmetric localization of Dvl3 during establishment of stereocilia orientation is consistent with the asymmetric localization of Dvl2 [6] and other core PCP components in mammals [34],[57],[58]. The polarized asymmetric arrangement of PCP proteins in the fly wing is also required for the uniform orientation of hairs [59],[60]. The sensory hair cells in this region are surrounded by the cellular processes of various types of supporting cells and tight cell contacts are formed between the cells (reviewed in [32]). Dvl3 appears to be localized on the cellular boundary formed between the sensory hair cells and the projections of the supporting cells, making it difficult to determine whether it is expressed on the lateral side of the hair cell, or on the medial side of the supporting cell. Dvl2 has previously been shown to localize at the lateral side of the hair cell [6] and as our evidence suggests redundant functions for the Dvl proteins, it seems likely that Dvl3 is also expressed here.
###end p 80
###begin p 81
###xml 115 119 115 119 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 119 122 119 122 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 135 139 135 139 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 139 142 139 142 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 143 147 143 147 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 147 150 147 150 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 166 169 166 169 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
###xml 170 174 170 174 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 222 226 222 226 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 226 229 226 229 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 230 234 230 234 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 234 237 234 237 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 333 337 333 337 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 337 340 337 340 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 341 345 341 345 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 345 348 345 348 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 404 408 404 408 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 408 411 408 411 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 488 497 488 497 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2-EGFP</italic>
###xml 572 576 572 576 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 576 579 576 579 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 832 835 832 835 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
Redundancy between the three Dvls in the developing organ of Corti was implied from the similarity of phenotype in Dvl3-/- mutants and Dvl1-/-;Dvl2-/- double mutants [6],[38]. Further, a mild PCP phenotype was observed in Dvl2+/-;Dvl3+/- double heterozygotes, despite normal development in the single heterozygotes and the defect in Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- double mutants was much more severe than in the single Dvl3-/- mutant. Interestingly, despite redundancy between the Dvls, addition of the Dvl2-EGFP BAC transgene was not able to rescue the rotated stereocilia phenotype in Dvl3-/- mutants. We again propose that a certain threshold of Dvl protein level may be required for normal development and the relative expression levels of the three Dvls in the developing organ of Corti influences the cochlear phenotype and the ability of a Dvl transgene to rescue this phenotype.
###end p 81
###begin p 82
###xml 19 23 19 23 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 23 26 23 26 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 27 33 27 33 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 40 44 40 44 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 44 47 44 47 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 48 54 48 54 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 235 239 235 239 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 239 242 239 242 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 243 249 243 249 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 256 260 256 260 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 260 263 260 263 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 264 270 264 270 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp</italic>
###xml 306 319 306 319 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">LtapLp/LtapLp</italic>
###xml 398 401 398 401 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
###xml 433 437 433 437 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 442 446 442 446 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 496 500 496 500 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 500 503 500 503 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 504 508 504 508 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 508 511 508 511 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
Interestingly, the Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ and Dvl3-/-;LtapLp/+ mutants that showed the CE/PCP-phenotype in the neural tube also displayed the PCP-phenotype in the organ of Corti. However, the misorientation phenotype was less severe in both Dvl3+/-;LtapLp/+ and Dvl3-/-;LtapLp/+ mutants than previously found in LtapLp/LtapLp mutants, in which 95% cells in the two outer hair cell rows are misorientated [6], possibly due to the remaining Dvl1 and Dvl2 alleles in these mutants. It was also noted that Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants with defects in the neural tube had a much more severe phenotype in the organ of Corti than those with normal neurulation, indicating a strong correlation between the PCP-phenotypes in these two tissues.
###end p 82
###begin p 83
###xml 35 39 35 39 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 44 48 44 48 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 144 148 144 148 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Hamblet1">[40]</xref>
###xml 192 195 192 195 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 232 236 232 236 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 236 239 236 239 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 551 555 551 555 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 555 558 555 558 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 559 563 559 563 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 563 566 563 566 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 646 650 646 650 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvls</italic>
###xml 790 795 790 795 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt3a</italic>
###xml 809 812 809 812 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">neo</sup>
###xml 804 812 804 812 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt3a<sup>neo</sup></italic>
###xml 814 818 814 818 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Takada1">[61]</xref>
###xml 875 880 875 880 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt3a</italic>
###xml 896 910 896 910 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">vestigial tail</italic>
###xml 982 986 982 986 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Greco1">[62]</xref>
###xml 1001 1006 1001 1006 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt5a</italic>
###xml 1073 1077 1073 1077 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 1077 1080 1077 1080 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1081 1085 1081 1085 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 1085 1088 1085 1088 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1166 1170 1166 1170 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Yamaguchi2">[63]</xref>
###xml 1541 1544 1541 1544 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 117 121 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 240 244 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 763 767 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 988 992 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">Mice</span>
We have previously shown that both Dvl1 and Dvl2 play roles in somite segregation, causing skeletal malformations in mice that lack these genes [40]. Given the high homology between the three Dvl genes, we examined the skeletons of Dvl3-/- mice. However, no vertebral or rib malformations were observed. Some mutants did display xiphoid bifurication, although we are unsure of the significance of this phenotype as it was also seen in several wild type controls. Severe skeletal defects involving truncation of the A-P axis were, however, observed in Dvl2-/-;Dvl3+/- double mutants, supporting previous evidence to suggest redundant roles of the Dvls in somite formation. A similar phenotype of lack of caudal somites and absence of tail bud formation is seen in mice homozygous for a null Wnt3a allele (Wnt3aneo) [61], and a less severe phenotype appears in the hypomorphic Wnt3a allele mutant, vestigial tail, which shows loss of caudal vertebrae causing a shortening of the tail [62]. Mice lacking Wnt5a are also shortened along the A-P axis with a phenotype similar to Dvl2+/-;Dvl3-/- mutants, and share outgrowth defects in the developing face and lack of tail [63]. Wnt3a is classically considered to stimulate canonical Wnt signals, whereas Wnt5a is normally associated with non-canonical Wnt mechanisms, indicating that further investigation is needed to determine which pathway or pathways Dvl is required to signal through for the normal development of these structures. We grossly examined Wnt signaling in both single and double Dvl mutants using the TOPflash reporter of TCF activity. Interestingly we found that global Wnt signaling was largely unaffected in even the most severely affected mutants, suggesting that only a low level of Dvl is sufficient for functional canonical Wnt signals. However, our data also suggests subtle abnormalities in Wnt signaling. Precise determination of these abnormalities will require careful sectioning of specific tissues and examination of various cell types throughout development.
###end p 83
###begin p 84
###xml 571 574 571 574 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
###xml 575 579 575 579 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 580 584 580 584 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Hamblet1">[40]</xref>
The three highly homologous Dvl proteins shared in mammals have very similar broad expression patterns in development. This study completes the initial characterization of the specific, individual roles of each of these proteins and also establishes functional redundancy and overlap in a number of developmental processes. Dvl3 is required for the development of the cardiac outflow tract and signals in the PCP pathway to regulate CE in the developing neural tube and cochlea, as well as cell polarity in the organ of Corti. Dvl1 and Dvl2 are redundant with each other [6],[38],[40] as well as with Dvl3 in a number of these developmental processes.
###end p 84

###end title 85

###xml 195 203 195 203 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt1-Cre</italic>

###xml 338 342 338 342 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 342 345 342 345 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>

###xml 390 400 390 400 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000259.s001">Figures S1</xref>
###xml 405 407 405 407 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="supplementary-material" rid="pgen.1000259.s002">S2</xref>
###xml 441 445 441 445 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 496 500 496 500 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 509 536 509 536 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="gene">5&#8242;-TCCGATGAGGATGATTCCACC-3&#8242;</named-content>
###xml 538 542 538 542 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 551 579 551 579 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="gene">5&#8242;-TGAGGCACTGCTCTGTTCTGT -3&#8242;</named-content>
###xml 581 585 581 585 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 595 623 595 623 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="gene">5&#8242;-TTGGCCCACAATGGAGATGCCC-3&#8242;</named-content>
###xml 631 634 631 634 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">neo</italic>
###xml 643 673 643 673 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="gene">5&#8242;-AGGCTTACCCGCTTCCATTGCTCA-3&#8242;</named-content>
###xml 747 751 747 751 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 781 807 781 807 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="gene">5&#8242;-GGACGCAGGAGATCTTTGAA-3&#8242;</named-content>
###xml 829 855 829 855 <named-content xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" content-type="gene">5&#8242;-CATAGCTGGGGTTGAAGCTC-3&#8242;</named-content>
###xml 1055 1059 1055 1059 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl1</italic>
###xml 1059 1063 1059 1063 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Lijam2">[41]</xref>
###xml 1065 1069 1065 1069 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2</italic>
###xml 1069 1073 1069 1073 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Hamblet1">[40]</xref>
###xml 1075 1084 1075 1084 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl2-EYFP</italic>
###xml 1095 1098 1095 1098 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang1">[6]</xref>
###xml 1100 1108 1100 1108 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt1-Cre</italic>
###xml 1108 1112 1108 1112 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Danielian1">[64]</xref>
###xml 1114 1122 1114 1122 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Isl1-Cre</italic>
###xml 1122 1126 1122 1126 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Cai1">[18]</xref>
###xml 1128 1144 1128 1144 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Rosa-26-lacZ Cre</italic>
###xml 1144 1148 1144 1148 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Soriano1">[65]</xref>
###xml 1153 1160 1153 1160 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">BAT-gal</italic>
###xml 1160 1164 1160 1164 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Maretto1">[66]</xref>
###xml 204 208 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 270 274 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 360 365 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mouse</span>
###xml 1009 1014 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mouse</span>
All animal care and experiments were performed under protocols approved by the NHGRI/NIH and UCSD Animal Care and Use Committees. LtapLp mutants were originally acquired from Jackson Laboratory, Wnt1-Cre mice were a kind gift of Dr. Andrew McMahon, Harvard and Isl1-Cre mice were a generous gift from Sylvia Evans, UCSD. We generated the Dvl3-/- and Dvl3-EYFP mouse mutants as described in Figures S1 and S2, respectively. Genotyping of the Dvl3 mutants was performed with the following primers, Dvl3 forward 5'-TCCGATGAGGATGATTCCACC-3', Dvl3 reverse 5'-TGAGGCACTGCTCTGTTCTGT -3', Dvl3 knockout 5'-TTGGCCCACAATGGAGATGCCC-3', NLpgk neo forward 5'-AGGCTTACCCGCTTCCATTGCTCA-3'. The PCR primers used to distinguish between the transgene and wild type Dvl3 allele were Dvl3lnt2 forward 5'-GGACGCAGGAGATCTTTGAA-3' and Dvl3Int2 reverse 5'-CATAGCTGGGGTTGAAGCTC-3' which amplify a band of 155 bp for the wild type allele and 189 bp for the transgene, due to the presence of the LoxP site. Genotyping for the following mouse mutants have previously been described; Dvl1[41], Dvl2[40], Dvl2-EYFP transgene [6], Wnt1-Cre[64], Isl1-Cre[18], Rosa-26-lacZ Cre[65] and BAT-gal[66].
###end p 87
###begin title 88
Scanning Electron Microscopy
###end title 88
###begin p 89
After fixing in 3% aldehyde solution (1.5% paraformaldehyde, 1.5% glutaraldehyde) in 0.1 M phosphate buffer pH 7.5, E18.5 hearts were stored in 100% ethanol following dehydration through a graded ethanol series. Hearts were critically point dried, mounted and coated with 300 Angstrom gold-palladium. A Cambridge Instrument Stereoscan 360 scanning electron microscope (Scripps Institute of Oceanography Analytical Facility) was used to view the prepared samples.
###end p 89
###begin title 90
Histology
###end title 90
###begin p 91
P0 hearts were dissected into 10% buffered formalin, dehydrated, embedded in paraffin wax, sectioned at 8 microm thickness and stained with hematoxylin and eosin using standard methods.
###end p 91
###begin p 92
###xml 45 49 45 49 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 49 52 49 52 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 61 65 61 65 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 65 68 65 68 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 83 91 83 91 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt1-Cre</italic>
###xml 91 95 91 95 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Danielian1">[64]</xref>
###xml 100 108 100 108 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Isl1-Cre</italic>
###xml 108 112 108 112 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Cai1">[18]</xref>
###xml 146 150 146 150 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 150 153 150 153 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">+/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 172 188 172 188 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Rosa-26-lacZ Cre</italic>
###xml 203 207 203 207 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Soriano1">[65]</xref>
###xml 657 658 641 642 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 69 73 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 154 158 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
To label the CNC and SHF cell populations in Dvl3-/- hearts, Dvl3+/- mice carrying Wnt1-Cre[64] and Isl1-Cre[18], respectively, were crossed with Dvl3+/- mice carrying the Rosa-26-lacZ Cre reporter gene [65]. Hearts dissected from embryos collected at E14.5 and E18.5 were stored in 30% sucrose in PBS at 4degreesC overnight, and then embedded in 7.5% gelatin, 15% sucrose. Sections (20 microm) were cut at -24degreesC on a cryostat and fixed in 2% formaldehyde, 0.2% glutaraldehyde, 0.02% NP-40 and 0.01% sodium deoxycholate. After washing, the slides were stained with 1 mg/ml X-gal in 35 mM potassium ferrocyanide, 35 mM potassium ferricyanide, 2 mM MgCl2, 0.02% NP-40, 0.01% sodium deoxycholate at 37degreesC overnight. After re-fixing in 4% paraformaldehyde, the slides were counterstained with Nuclear Fast Red (Vector Lab), according to the manufacturer's protocol. Whole embryos from the above crosses were also collected at E10.5 and stained for beta-galactosidase activity using the same procedures. All images were captured using a Spot 2 camera mounted on a Leica DMR light microscope.
###end p 92
###begin p 93
###xml 38 41 38 41 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl</italic>
###xml 90 97 90 97 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">BAT-gal</italic>
###xml 112 116 112 116 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Maretto1">[66]</xref>
###xml 49 53 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 72 76 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
To visualize canonical Wnt signaling, Dvl mutant mice were crossed with mice carrying the BAT-gal reporter gene [66] and embryos collected at various stages of development. Staining for beta-galactosidase activity was performed as described above.
###end p 93
###begin title 94
Confocal Microscopy
###end title 94
###begin p 95
###xml 30 39 30 39 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3-EYFP</italic>
To visualize Dvl3 expression, Dvl3-EYFP embryos or cochleae were fixed in 4% paraformaldehyde for 30 minutes or overnight at 4degreesC. To examine the stereocilia in the sensory hair cells, organs of Corti were stained with fluorescein- rhodamine-conjugated phalloidin (Molecular Probes). Both native YFP signal and fluorescent staining was observed using an Olympus FV 1000 or a Zeiss LSM 510 confocal scanning microscope.
###end p 95
###begin title 96
Patterning Defect Quantification in the Cochlea
###end title 96
###begin p 97
To measure the severity of the patterning defect, the whole cochlea duct was scanned and the cells numbered for length reference. The number of cells in the defective regions (where there were no longer three outer hair cell rows) was then calculated as a percentage of total cells.
###end p 97
###begin title 98
Supporting Information
###end title 98
###begin p 99
###xml 38 42 38 42 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 61 65 61 65 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 171 175 171 175 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Yang1">[13]</xref>
###xml 177 181 177 181 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 287 291 287 291 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 496 500 496 500 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Tybulewicz1">[67]</xref>
###xml 661 665 661 665 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Deng1">[68]</xref>
###xml 1267 1271 1267 1271 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Deng1">[68]</xref>
###xml 1274 1275 1274 1275 <sub xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">2</sub>
###xml 1336 1339 1336 1339 <sup xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">&#8722;/&#8722;</sup>
###xml 1332 1339 1332 1339 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3<sup>&#8722;/&#8722;</sup></italic>
###xml 1523 1530 1523 1530 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">methods</xref>
###xml 53 57 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
###xml 700 704 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
Targeted disruption and generation of Dvl3 deficient mice. A Dvl3 genomic clone was isolated from a 129 genomic DNA library in FIX II (Stratagene) as previously described [13]. Dvl3 genomic fragments were subcloned into pBluescript KS II (Stratagene) to enable efficient generation of a Dvl3 knock-out construct (A). A 3.6 kb BamH-Bgl2 fragment from within intron 1 to the middle of exon 2 and a 2.5 kb Dra1-Not1 (from vector MCS) fragment from within intron 7 to beyond 13 were cloned into pPNT [67] either side of the neomycin resistance gene and in the opposite direction to this marker (A). Gene targeting of this construct in TC1 embryonic stem (ES) cells [68] was used to generate the knockout mice and individual clones were selected and screened by Dra1 digest of genomic DNA with the 3' probe. Correct targeting of clone 72 (1 of 100 clones) resulted in the presence of a 7.8 Kb targeted allele and a 6 Kb wildtype allele (B). To confirm homologous recombination, a 5' probe was used to detect a 5 Kb fragment in Nco1 digested ES clone genomic DNA (B). This correctly targeted clone was injected and successfully transmitted through germline. Lines were established in both mixed (129S6xNIH Black Swiss) and uniform (129S6) genetic backgrounds, as described [68]. F2 litters contained wild type and heterozygous offspring. Dvl3-/- embryos were collected from crosses between heterozygotes and western blot analysis using E13.5 whole embryo lysates confirmed the absence of Dvl3 protein (C). PCR primers (listed in methods) were designed to distinguish wild type, heterozygous and homozygous genotypes (D).
###end p 99

###end p 100

###end p 101
###begin p 102
###xml 26 30 26 30 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 57 61 57 61 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 154 158 154 158 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Wang3">[38]</xref>
###xml 201 205 201 205 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 419 423 419 423 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="bibr" rid="pgen.1000259-Lee2">[69]</xref>
###xml 523 527 523 527 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 824 831 824 831 <xref xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" ref-type="sec" rid="s4">methods</xref>
###xml 960 964 960 964 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Dvl3</italic>
###xml 643 648 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mouse</span>
Generation of EYFP-tagged Dvl3 transgene. An EYFP-tagged Dvl3 transgene was generated using homologous recombination of BACs (A), as described previously [38]. Briefly, BAC clones containing the whole Dvl3 genomic region, including flanking sequences, were identified using overlapping PCR primers covering the entire region from a BAC library (Genome Systems). BAC modifications were performed as previously described [69], using a SacB-Neo selection cassette (A). An EYFP cassette was fused in-frame to the last codon of Dvl3 and LoxP sites were introduced within intron 2 and the 3' UTR flanking region. Western blot analysis of transgenic mouse E13.5 embryo lysates was used to confirm expression of the transgene, which was larger than the wild type Dvl3 protein due to the additional EYFP (3B). PCR primers (listed in methods) binding either side of the LoxP site in intron2 (red arrows in A) were used to distinguish between the transgene and wild type Dvl3 allele (C).
###end p 102

(3.8 MB TIF)
###end p 103

###xml 97 105 97 105 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Wnt1-Cre</italic>
###xml 136 146 136 146 <italic xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" xmlns:mml="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">Islet1-Cre</italic>
###xml 106 110 <span type="species:ncbi:10090">mice</span>
